            <div class="td-module-meta-info">
                <span class="td-post-author-name"><a href="http://www.theindependentmedia.org/author/daanishsheikh/">Danish Sheikh</a> <span>-</span> </span>                <span class="td-post-date"><time class="entry-date updated td-module-date" datetime="2017-02-20T21:34:42+00:00" >20th February 2017</time></span>                <div class="td-module-comments"><a href="http://www.theindependentmedia.org/mark-zuckerburg-says-he-has-a-vision-for-a-global-network/#respond">0</a></div>            </div>


            <div class="td-excerpt">
                To say it’s a utopian vision would be an understatement.
